(U-Haul), Amerco Real Estate Company (Real Estate), Republic Western Insurance Company (Republic) Oxford Life Insurance Company (Oxford). Throughout Form 10-K, context requires, term "AMERCO" includes subsidiaries. AMERCO's executive offices located 1325 Airmotive Way, Suite 100, Reno, Nevada 89502-3239, telephone number (775) 688-6300. As Form 10-K, references fiscal year refer AMERCO's fiscal year ended March 31 year. Republic Oxford consolidated basis calendar years ended December 31. Accordingly, references years 1999, 1998 1997 correspond AMERCO's fiscal years 2000, 1999 1998, respectively. AMERCO industry segments represented Moving Storage Operations (U-Haul), Real Estate, Property Casualty Insurance (Republic) Life Insurance (Oxford). See Note 21 Notes Consolidated Financial Statements Item 8 financial information industry segments. Operations conducted registered tradename U-Haul<REGISTERED TRADEMARK> United States Canada. Real Estate responsible managing properties including environmental risks properties. Real Estate responsible purchase properties AMERCO subsidiaries. Real Estate handles dispositions (sale lease) unused real estate. On November 21, 1997, Oxford purchased issued outstanding shares Encore Financial, Inc. subsidiaries (Encore). Encore's primary subsidiary North American Insurance Company (NAI). NAI's premium volume primarily sale credit life disability products, Medicare supplement insurance. NAI owns issued outstanding common shares North American Fire & Casualty Insurance Company (NAFCIC), property casualty company. In December 1998, NAFCIC sold Republic. On November 24, 1997, Oxford purchased issued outstanding shares Safe Mate Life Insurance Company (Safe Mate). As November 1, 1998, Safe Mate merged Oxford. Safe Mate's business sale credit life disability products. B. HISTORY U-Haul founded 1945 "U-Haul Trailer Rental Company". From 1945 1974, U-Haul rented trailers and, starting 1959, trucks one-way In-Town<REGISTERED TRADEMARK> basis independent dealers. Since 1974, U-Haul developed network owned rental centers (U-Haul Centers) U-Haul rents trucks trailers related products services (e.g., sale installation hitches, sale boxes moving supplies). At March 31, 2000, U-Haul's distribution network included 1,200 U-Haul Centers 14,500 independent dealers. <PAGE> 4 C. MOVING STORAGE OPERATIONS Business Strategies The U-Haul business strategy remains focused do-it-yourself moving self-storage customers. U-Haul believes customer access, terms truck trailer availability proximity rental locations, critical success. Under U-Haul name, strategy offer, integrated manner extensive geographically diverse network 15,700 Company-owned Centers independent dealers, wide range products services do-it- moving self-storage customers. Moving Operations U-Haul variety product offerings. Rental trucks designed do-it-yourself customers mind. U-Haul trailers suited low profile newly manufactured automobiles. As March 31, 2000, U-Haul rental equipment fleet consisted 97,000 trucks, 80,300 trailers 19,200 tow dollies. Additionally, U-Haul support rental items furniture pads bumper hitches. Approximately 90% U-Haul's rental revenue do-it-yourself movers. Moving rentals include: (i) In-Town<REGISTERED TRADEMARK> rentals, equipment returned originating U-Haul location (ii) one-way rentals, equipment returned U-Haul location city. U-Haul's truck trailer rental business seasonal, proportionally transactions revenues generated spring summer months balance year. U-Haul sells wide selection moving supplies include boxes, tape packaging materials. U-Haul Centers sell install hitches towing systems, sell propane. U-Haul offers protection packages as: (i) Safemove<REGISTERED TRADEMARK> - moving customers damage waiver, cargo protection medical life coverage (ii) Safestor<REGISTERED TRADEMARK> - self-storage rental customers types protection goods storage. Independent dealers receive U-Haul equipment consignment basis paid commission gross revenues generated rentals. U-Haul maintains contracts independent dealers typically terminated 30 days written notice party. U-Haul designs manufactures truck van boxes, trailers support rental equipment items. Truck chassis manufactured foreign domestic truck manufacturers. These chassis receive post-delivery modifications joined van boxes strategically located Company-owned manufacturing assembly facilities United States. U-Haul services maintains trucks trailers extensive preventive-maintenance program, generally performed Company- owned facilities located U-Haul Centers. Major repairs performed chassis manufacturers' dealers Company- owned repair shops, U-Haul takes advantage manufacturers' warranties. Competition The moving truck trailer rental market highly competitive dominated national operators In-Town<REGISTERED TRADEMARK> one-way markets. Recently major competitors combined. Budget Rent-A-Car acquired Ryder TRS (Ryder Truck Rentals). Management believes merger material adverse effect AMERCO's financial position operating results. Management believes distinct users rental trucks: commercial users do-it-yourself users. U-Haul focuses do-it-yourself mover. U-Haul believes principal competitive factors convenience rental locations, availability quality rental equipment price. <PAGE> 5 Self-Storage Business U-Haul entered self-storage business 1974 increased rentable square footage storage locations acquisition existing facilities construction. Ten percent U-Haul's rental revenue generated storage. In addition, U-Haul entered management agreements manage self-storage properties owned others. U-Haul entered strategic financial partnership Private Mini Storage Realty, L.P., Texas-based operator self-storage properties. Through 900 owned managed storage locations United States Canada, U-Haul offers rent 29.1 million square feet self-storage space. U-Haul's self-storage facility locations range sizes 152,000 square feet storage space, individual storage units sizes 15 square feet 400 square feet. The primary market storage rooms storage household goods. With addition 20,000 storage rooms fiscal year 2000, average occupancy rate facilities operating year 84.1%, modest seasonal variations. During fiscal year 2000, delinquent rentals percentage total storage rentals approximately 6.8%. U-Haul considers rate satisfactory. Competition The primary competition U-Haul self-storage location storage facilities trade area offering comparable level convenience customer. COMPLIANCE SECTION 414(U) CODE..............-84- <PAGE> AMERCO EMPLOYEE SAVINGS, PROFIT SHARING EMPLOYEE OWNERSHIP PLAN PREAMBLE INTRODUCTION ------------------------- On March 16, 1973, AMERCO, Nevada corporation (the "Corporation") established AMERCO Profit Sharing Retirement Trust (the "Profit Sharing Plan") employees. The Profit Sharing Plan subsequently amended time time. Effective April 1, 1984, Corporation established AMERCO Employee Savings Protection Plan (the "Savings Plan") permit employee contributions made favorable tax basis utilization provisions Section 401(k) Internal Revenue Code (the "Code"). The Savings Plan subsequently amended time time. Effective January 1, 1988, Profit Sharing Plan Savings Plan merged single plan called "AMERCO Retirement Savings Profit Sharing Plan" (the "Plan"). The Plan amended restated entirety, effective July 24, 1988, establish "employee stock ownership plan" (as defined Section 407(d)(6) Employee Retirement Income Security Act 1974 (the "Act") Section 4975(e)(7) Code) designed invest primarily "qualifying employer securities" (as defined Section 407(d)(5) Act Section 4975(e)(8) Code) Corporation. The July 24, 1988, restatement changed Plan "AMERCO Employee Savings, Profit Sharing And Employee Stock Ownership Plan." The Plan subsequently amended restated entirety effective January 1, 1989 comply Tax Reform Act 1986 ("TRA 86") make modifications. The Plan amended occasions. By adoption document, Plan amended restated entirety comply Small Business Job Protection Act 1996 ("SBJPA"), Uniformed Services Employment Reemployment Rights Act 1994 ("USERRA"), Taxpayer Relief Act 1997 ("TRA 97") make modifications. It intention Corporation Plan continue qualified provisions Section 401(a) Code Trust Fund maintained pursuant Plan continue exempt taxation pursuant Section 501(a) Code. The Plan amended qualified profit sharing plan "cash deferred" feature Section 401(k) Code, constituent employee stock ownership plan feature. The provisions Plan apply Participant termination employment occurs Effective Date provisions. <PAGE> ARTICLE ----------- EFFECTIVE -------------- 1.1. EFFECTIVE DATE. -------------- Except specifically provided respect provision Plan required SBJPA, USERRA TRA 97, provisions amended restated Plan effective January 1, 1997.
